Upon assessment, the patient's s/s are consistent with status past L ORIF of radius. Patient presents with moderate swelling
and severe limitations in ROM, mobility, and decreased arthrokinematics of elbow and wrist five weeks post op, Concerns

and would benefit from skilled physical therapy to address deficits listed above. The patlent was educated on and is in

unable to move her fingers well secondary to swelling and N/T Into 3-4 finger going up into the outside of her elbow. She is now
sleeping inher bed but has been sleeping onthe couch due to discomfort.

Assessment
Assessment
The pleasant 33y/o female patient appears before physical therapy this date with reports of L wrist stiffness, loss of ROM,
decreased use for ADL's and IADL's secondary to decreased dexterity and strength, as well as N/T in ulnar aspect distribution.
Upon assessment, the patient's s/s are consistent with status post L ORIF of radius, Patient presents with moderate swelling
and severe limitations in ROM, mobility, and decreased arthrokinematics of elbow and wrist five weeks post op. Concerns
regarding end ranges of elbow flexion, supination, as well as global mobility of MCP’s + wrist. The patient is appropriate for
and would benefit from skilled physical therapy to address deficits listed above. The patient was educated onand is in
agreement with the goals established and the physical therapy plan of care to ensue. The patient consents to physical therapy
treatment. There are no contraindications to beginning physical therapy atthis time.
Prognosis
Good potential to reach and maintain prior level of function
